\DoxyCodeLine{01946 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{01947     \textcolor{comment}{/* https://bottosson.github.io/posts/oklab/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01948 \textcolor{comment}{       https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oklab\_color\_space */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01949     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} R\_255, G\_255, B\_255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01950     \mbox{\hyperlink{Almog__Draw__Library_8h_a1e38982ab1aaaae615016576f660dff1}{HexARGB\_RGB\_VAR}}(hex\_ARGB, R\_255, G\_255, B\_255);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01951 }
\DoxyCodeLine{01952     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} R = R\_255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01953     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} G = G\_255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01954     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} B = B\_255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01955 }
\DoxyCodeLine{01956     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} l = 0.4122214705f * R + 0.5363325363f * G + 0.0514459929f * B;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01957     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} m = 0.2119034982f * R + 0.6806995451f * G + 0.1073969566f * B;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01958     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} s = 0.0883024619f * R + 0.2817188376f * G + 0.6299787005f * B;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01959 }
\DoxyCodeLine{01960     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} l\_ = cbrtf(l);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01961     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} m\_ = cbrtf(m);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01962     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} s\_ = cbrtf(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01963 }
\DoxyCodeLine{01964     *L = 0.2104542553f * l\_ + 0.7936177850f * m\_ -\/ 0.0040720468f * s\_;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01965     *a = 1.9779984951f * l\_ -\/ 2.4285922050f * m\_ + 0.4505937099f * s\_;}
\DoxyCodeLine{01966     *b = 0.0259040371f * l\_ + 0.7827717662f * m\_ -\/ 0.8086757660f * s\_;}
